     <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function() {
		    // search focus
    		$('#search_main input[id=search]').focus();

    		// header
    		$('.nav-links-main').clone().removeClass('nav-links nav-links-main').addClass('nav-links-clone nav-links-clone-main').prependTo('nav.nav-links-clone-wrapper');
    		$('.nav-links-tertiary .tertiary').clone().removeClass('nav-links nav-links-tertiary').addClass('nav-links-clone').appendTo('.nav-links-clone');
    		$('html').click(function() {
				$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper, .more-tertiary-links').slideUp();
				$('.nav-links-toggle, .tertiary-more-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
				$('.tertiary-more').removeClass('active');
			});
			$('.nav-links-toggle, .tertiary-more-toggle').click(function(event){
				event.stopPropagation();
			});
	    	$('.nav-links-toggle').click(function() {
	    		if($('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').is(':hidden')) {
	    			$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').slideDown();
	    			$('.nav-links-toggle').addClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
	    		} else {
	    			$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').slideUp();
	    			$('.nav-links-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
	    		}
	    	});
	    	$('.tertiary-more-toggle').click(function() {
	    		if ($('.more-tertiary-links').is(':visible')) {
	    			$('.more-tertiary-links').slideUp();
	    			$('.tertiary-more').removeClass('active');
	    			$('.tertiary-more-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
	    		} else {
	    			$('.more-tertiary-links').slideDown();
	    			$('.tertiary-more').addClass('active');
	    			$('.tertiary-more-toggle').addClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
	    		}
	    	});
	    	$(window).on("load resize scroll",function(e){
	    		$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').hide();
				$('.nav-links-toggle, .tertiary-more-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
				$('.tertiary-more').removeClass('active');
				$('.more-tertiary-links').slideUp();
	    	});
		    $('.h_account').tooltip();
		});
     </script>
    </header>

        <p>
         <span class="mute">
          March 1, 2021 by Margaret Wood
         </span>
         <br/>
         <strong>
          Congress.gov New, Tip and Top for March 2021, Part 1
         </strong>
         <br/>
         Last month, Robert provided news of two enhancements to Congress.gov. The first involved new email alerts for committee profile
         <a href="https://blogs.loc.gov/law/2021/03/congress-gov-new-tip-and-top-for-march-2021-part-1/">
          ...more
         </a>
        </p>

        <h2>
         The Legislative Process
        </h2>
        <div class="img_holder margin-bottom-small">
         <img alt="Legislative Process video" height="148" src="https://www.congress.gov/img/video-legislative-process.jpg" width="204"/>
        </div>
        <p class="margin-bottom-medium">
         <a href="/legislative-process">
          Nine videos
         </a>
         explain each of the common legislative stages, and that the process by which a bill becomes law is rarely predictable.
        </p>

         <a href="https://www.congress.gov/content/legprocess/legislative-process-poster.jpg" target="_blank">
          JPG (179 KB)
         </a>

        <h2>
         About Congress.gov
        </h2>

        </p>

    <div class="top-link">
     <a href="#" id="sticky-back-to-top">
      <i>
      </i>
      <span>
       Back to top
      </span>
     </a>
    </div>
    <script type="text/javascript">
     $(function () {
        var scroll_timer,
            displayed = false,
            $message = $('.top-link a').hide(),
            $window = $(window),
            top = $(document.body).children(0).position().top;

        $("#sticky-back-to-top").click(function(event){
            $window.scrollTop(0);
            event.preventDefault();
            return false;
        });

        $window.scroll(function () {
            window.clearTimeout(scroll_timer);
            scroll_timer = window.setTimeout(function () {
                if($window.scrollTop() <= top){
                    displayed = false;
                    $message.fadeOut(800);
                }else if(displayed == false){
                    displayed = true;
                    $message.stop(true, true).show().click(function () { $message.fadeOut(800); });
                }
            }, 100);
        });
    });
    </script>
   </footer>
   <!-- end footer -->

   </script>
   <script src="/js/map/mapSearchWidget.js">
   </script>

   <div class="actionLoader">
    <i class="fas fa-circle-notch fa-spin fa-3x fa-fw">
    </i>
    <span class="sr-only">
     Loading...
    </span>
   </div>
  </div>
  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
        // Display system alert if not empty, suppress borwser support warning if present
        if ($('#system_alert').is(':not(:empty)')) {
            $('#system_alert').removeAttr("style").prepend('<span class="hide_fromsighted">Alert: </span>');
            $('#browser_support_alert').attr("style","display:none");
        }

        var h = window.location.hash,
            scrollTo = 0;

        if (h) {
            if ($(h).offset() !== undefined) {
                scrollTo = $(h).offset().top;
            }
        }

        if (scrollTo > 0) {
            $('html, body').stop().animate({ scrollTop : scrollTo + "px"}, 0);
        }

        $('body').congress_LAC({ checkUrl: '/lac/check' });
    });
  </script>
